*Grade 1 Maths — October Quiz*
_2255 questions (1755 new + 500 revision)_

*Q1.* 🍇 Pari had 79 grapes and gave 6 away. How many grapes left?
A) 72
B) 74
C) 79
D) 73
✅ *Answer:* D) 73
💡 79 - 6 = 73 grapes left.
